NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING CHANGE
OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES WILL
REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
G. Prakash was born as a male child to S. Ganesan on 12-05-1973, residing at No. 3/2A, Rail Nagar, Tanjai Main
Road, Tiruchirappalli District. After an elaborate Sexual reassignment surgery she has been living as a Transgender
(Reference Dr. Samsath Begum, M.B.B.S., DGO, Tiruchirappalli District). The Thorough clinical Examination under
Dr. Samsath Begum, M.B.B.S., DGO, Tiruchirappalli shows that I could be treated as a female, Hence G. Prakash shall
be known as Transgender KAJOL.
Tiruchirappalli,
16th July 2012.

G. PRAKASH.

M. Saravanakumar was born as a male child to V. Maran on 21-06-1989 residing at No. 107/NA, Barathydasan Street,
Thuvakudi Malai, Thiruverambur, Tiruchirappalli District, After an elaborate Sexual reassignment surgery she has been
living as a Transgender (Reference Dr. Samsath Begum, M.B.B.S., DGO, Tiruchirappalli District). The Thorough clinical
Examination under Dr. Samsath Begum, M.B.B.S., DGO, Tiruchirappalli shows that I could be treated as a female, Hence
M. SARAVANAKUMAR shall be known as Transgender SANIYA.
Tiruchirappalli,
16th July 2012.

M. SARAVANAKUMAR.
